## Diagram 2

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Conditional: Helm Values Check
    Conditional --> CreateClusterRole: rbac.install = true
    Conditional --> Skip: rbac.install = false
    CreateClusterRole --> DefineMetadata
    DefineMetadata --> SetLabels
    SetLabels --> DefineRules
    DefineRules --> SetAPIGroups
    SetAPIGroups --> SetResources
    SetResources --> SetVerbs
    SetVerbs --> [*]
    Skip --> [*]
```
